-- Name: assign_order_id_to_orderdetail(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres

CREATE FUNCTION public.assign_order_id_to_orderdetail() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id INT;
BEGIN
  -- Lấy order_id mới nhất (ưu tiên pending)
  SELECT order_id
  INTO v_order_id
  FROM customerorder
  WHERE status = 'pending'
  ORDER BY order_id DESC
  LIMIT 1;

  IF v_order_id IS NULL THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Không có order pending nào để gán vào orderdetail';
  END IF;

  NEW.order_id := v_order_id;
  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.assign_order_id_to_orderdetail() OWNER TO postgres;

CREATE FUNCTION public.create_order_for_new_customer() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
DECLARE
    v_order_id INTEGER; -- Biến để lưu order_id mới tạo
BEGIN
    -- Tạo đơn hàng mới với customer_id từ khách vừa nhập
    INSERT INTO customerorder (customer_id, status, order_date, total_price)
    VALUES (NEW.customer_id, 'pending', NOW(), 0)
    RETURNING order_id INTO v_order_id;
    
    -- Trả về giá trị vừa tạo
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.create_order_for_new_customer() OWNER TO postgres;

-- Name: decrease_product_quantity(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.decrease_product_quantity() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
BEGIN
    -- Kiểm tra nếu số lượng sản phẩm còn đủ
    IF (SELECT quantity FROM product WHERE cake_id = NEW.cake_id) >= NEW.quantity THEN
        -- Giảm số lượng sản phẩm trong bảng product
        UPDATE product
        SET quantity = quantity - NEW.quantity
        WHERE cake_id = NEW.cake_id;
    ELSE
        RAISE EXCEPTION 'Không đủ số lượng sản phẩm trong kho!';
    END IF;
    
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.decrease_product_quantity() OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- TOC entry 249 (class 1255 OID 17096)
-- Name: insert_review_for_completed_order(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.insert_review_for_completed_order() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
BEGIN
    IF NEW.status = 'delivered' THEN
        INSERT INTO review (order_detail_id, customer_comment, rating)
        SELECT od.order_detail_id, '', NULL
        FROM orderdetail od
        WHERE od.order_id = NEW.order_id;
    END IF;
    
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.insert_review_for_completed_order() OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- TOC entry 250 (class 1255 OID 17097)
-- Name: restore_product_quantity(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.restore_product_quantity() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
BEGIN
    -- Kiểm tra nếu trạng thái đơn hàng là "canceled"
    IF NEW.status = 'canceled' THEN
        -- Khôi phục số lượng sản phẩm trong kho cho tất cả các sản phẩm trong đơn hàng
        UPDATE product p
        SET quantity = p.quantity + od.quantity
        FROM orderdetail od
        WHERE od.order_id = NEW.order_id AND p.cake_id = od.cake_id;
    END IF;
    
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.restore_product_quantity() OWNER TO postgres;

    LANGUAGE plpgsql

    WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;
    
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;

--
-- TOC entry 252 (class 1255 OID 17099)
-- Name: update_payment_status(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.update_payment_status() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
BEGIN
    IF NEW.status = 'delivered' THEN
        UPDATE payment
        SET payment_status = 'completed'
        WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;
    END IF;
    
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.update_payment_status() OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- TOC entry 253 (class 1255 OID 17100)
-- Name: update_sub_total(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.update_sub_total() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
BEGIN
    -- Lấy giá của sản phẩm từ bảng product
    UPDATE orderdetail
    SET sub_total = (SELECT p.price * NEW.quantity
                     FROM product p
                     WHERE p.cake_id = NEW.cake_id)
    WHERE order_detail_id = NEW.order_detail_id;
    
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.update_sub_total() OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- TOC entry 254 (class 1255 OID 17101)
-- Name: update_total_price(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.update_total_price() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
BEGIN
    -- Cập nhật tổng giá trị đơn hàng trong customerorder
    UPDATE customerorder
    SET total_price = (
        SELECT COALESCE(SUM(p.price * od.quantity), 0)
        FROM orderdetail od
        JOIN product p ON od.cake_id = p.cake_id
        WHERE od.order_id = NEW.order_id
    )
    WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;
    
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.update_total_price() OWNER TO postgres;

CREATE VIEW public.customer_cart_view AS
 SELECT c.customer_id,
    o.order_id,
    o.order_detail_id,
    c.order_date,
    o.quantity,
    p.cake_name,
    o.sub_total,
    c.total_price
   FROM ((public.product p

     JOIN public.customerorder c USING (order_id))
  WHERE (c.customer_id = (current_setting('my.customer_id'::text))::integer)
  ORDER BY o.order_detail_id;

CREATE VIEW public.customer_payment_view AS
 SELECT c.customer_id,
    (((c.first_name)::text || ' '::text) || (c.last_name)::text) AS fullname,

    payment.payment_status,
    payment.payment_date

     JOIN public.customer c USING (customer_id))
  WHERE (c.customer_id = (current_setting('my.customer_id'::text))::integer);

     JOIN public.optioncake o USING (option_cake_id));

--
-- TOC entry 239 (class 1259 OID 17163)
-- Name: view_available_cakes; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE VIEW public.view_available_cakes AS
 SELECT DISTINCT ON (p.cake_id) p.cake_name,
    p.description,
    p.price,
    o.category_name,
    p.quantity
   FROM (public.product p
     JOIN public.optioncake o USING (option_cake_id))
  WHERE (p.quantity > 0);


ALTER VIEW public.view_available_cakes OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- TOC entry 240 (class 1259 OID 17167)
-- Name: view_new_cakes_last_month; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE VIEW public.view_new_cakes_last_month AS
 SELECT p.cake_name,
    p.description,
    p.price,
    o.category_name,
    p.quantity,
    p.create_at
   FROM (public.product p
     JOIN public.optioncake o USING (option_cake_id))
  WHERE (p.create_at >= (now() - '1 mon'::interval))
  ORDER BY p.create_at DESC;


ALTER VIEW public.view_new_cakes_last_month OWNER TO postgres;

    r.created_at,

    r.customer_comment,
    r.rating
   FROM ((public.product p
     JOIN public.orderdetail o USING (cake_id))
     JOIN public.review r USING (order_detail_id));


ALTER VIEW public.view_review OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- TOC entry 244 (class 1259 OID 17183)
-- Name: view_top5_best_seller; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE VIEW public.view_top5_best_seller AS
 SELECT p.cake_name,
    p.description,
    p.price,
    o.category_name,
    sum(ord.quantity) AS total_sold
   FROM ((public.product p
     JOIN public.optioncake o USING (option_cake_id))
     JOIN public.orderdetail ord USING (cake_id))
  GROUP BY p.cake_id, p.cake_name, p.description, p.price, o.category_name
  ORDER BY (sum(ord.quantity)) DESC
 LIMIT 5;


ALTER VIEW public.view_top5_best_seller OWNER TO postgres;
